## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models population growth rate dP/dt as a function of population size P and time t, which is the fundamental problem of population dynamics. The relationship likely involves density-dependent growth mechanisms such as logistic growth, Allee effects, or time-varying carrying capacities.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent growth)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth rate decreasing logarithmically with population)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P * c1 - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth negative below critical threshold)
- Allee effect (weak): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (c2 + P) (reduced growth at low density without negative region)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (asymmetric sigmoidal growth)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (rational density dependence)
- Time-dependent Malthusian: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) (exponential growth with time-varying rate)
- Logistic with time-varying rate: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * exp(c2 * t) (logistic with environmental change)
- Power-law growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (fractional-order population dynamics)
- Hassell-type: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P)**c2 (generalized density-dependent competition)
- Von Bertalanffy-type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolism-catabolism balance)
- Polynomial density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (cubic density dependence)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent negative feedback → multiplicative factor (1 - c*P) or (1 - (c*P)**n) reducing growth at high population
- Allee effect (positive density dependence at low P) → additional multiplicative factor (P - c) or (c + P) creating growth reduction or sign change at low population
- Carrying capacity structure → dP/dt = 0 at specific nonzero P value, implying factorization with (K - P) type terms
- Gompertz-type logarithmic feedback → log(c/P) term indicating growth rate decreases logarithmically rather than linearly with density
- Rational density dependence → P/(1 + c*P) structure indicating contest-type competition where per-capita effects saturate
- Depensation / critical population threshold → cubic or higher-order polynomial in P with multiple real roots indicating unstable equilibria
- Time-explicit environmental forcing → multiplicative or additive periodic/exponential functions of t modulating intrinsic growth rate
- Metabolic scaling → fractional powers of P (e.g., P^(3/4)) reflecting allometric scaling of resource use with body/population size
